===============

================

Changelog
---------

### Tomcat 10.1.52 (schultz)

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 3: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69936](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69936): Fix bug in previous fix for Tomcat Native crashes on shutdown that triggered a significant memory leak. Patch provided by Wes. (markt) 

### not released Tomcat 10.1.51 (schultz)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 4: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69623](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69623): Additional fix for the long standing regression that meant that calls to `ClassLoader.getResource().getContent()` failed when made from within a web application with resource caching enabled if the target resource was packaged in a JAR file. (markt) 
*   ![Image 5: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Pull request [#923](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/923): Avoid adding multiple CSRF tokens to a URL in the `CsrfPreventionFilter`. (schultz) 
*   ![Image 6: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69918](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69918): Ensure request parameters are correctly parsed for HTTP/2 requests when the content-length header is not set. (dsoumis) 
*   ![Image 7: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Enable minimum and recommended Tomcat Native versions to be set separately for Tomcat Native 1.x and 2.x. Update the minimum and recommended versions for Tomcat Native 1.x to 1.3.4. Update the minimum and recommended versions for Tomcat Native 2.x to 2.0.12. (markt) 
*   ![Image 8: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add a new `ssoReauthenticationMode` to the Tomcat provided Authenticators that provides a per Authenticator override of the SSO Valve `requireReauthentication` attribute. (markt) 
*   ![Image 9: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure URL encoding errors in the Rewrite Valve trigger an exception rather than silently using a replacement character. (markt) 
*   ![Image 10: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69932](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69932): Fix request end access log pattern regression, which would log the start time of the request instead. (remm) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 11: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid possible NPEs when using a TLS enabled custom connector. (remm) 
*   ![Image 12: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve warnings when setting ciphers lists in the FFM code, mirroring the tomcat-native changes. (remm) 
*   ![Image 13: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69910](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69910): Dereference TLS objects right after closing a socket to improve memory efficiency. (remm) 
*   ![Image 14: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Relax the JSSE vs OpenSSL configuration style checks on `SSLHostConfig` to reflect the existing implementation that allows one configuration style to be used for the trust attributes and a different style for all the other attributes. (markt) 
*   ![Image 15: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Better warning message when `OpenSSLConf` configuration elements are used with a JSSE TLS implementation. (markt) 
*   ![Image 16: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) When using OpenSSL via FFM, don't log a warning about missing CA certificates unless CA certificates were configured and the configuration failed. (markt) 
*   ![Image 17: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) For configuration consistency between OpenSSL and JSSE TLS implementations, TLSv1.3 cipher suites included in the `ciphers` attribute of an `SSLHostConfig` are now always ignored (previously they would be ignored with OpenSSL implementations and used with JSSE implementations) and a warning is logged that the cipher suite has been ignored. (markt) 
*   ![Image 18: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add the `ciphersuite` attribute to `SSLHostConfig` to configure the TLSv1.3 cipher suites. (markt) 
*   ![Image 19: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add OCSP support to JSSE based TLS connectors and make the use of OCSP configurable per connector for both JSSE and OpenSSL based TLS implementations. Align the checks performed by OpenSSL with those performed by JSSE. (markt) 
*   ![Image 20: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for soft failure of OCSP checks with soft failure support disabled by default. (markt) 
*   ![Image 21: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for configuring the verification flags passed to `OCSP_basic_verify` when using an OpenSSL based TLS implementation. (markt) 
*   ![Image 22: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix OpenSSL FFM code compatibility with LibreSSL versions below 3.5. (remm) 
*   ![Image 23: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Prevent concurrent release of `OpenSSLEngine` resources and the termination of the Tomcat Native library as it can cause crashes during Tomcat shutdown. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 24: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69333](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69333): Correct a regression in the previous fix for [69333](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69333) and ensure that `reuse()` or `release()` is always called for a tag. (markt) 

#### Cluster

*   ![Image 25: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif)[62814](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=62814): Document that human-readable names may be used for `mapSendOptions` and align documentation with `channelSendOptions`. Based on pull request [#929](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/929) by archan0621. (markt) 

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 26: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69920](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69920): When attempting to write to a closed `Writer` or `OutputStream` obtained from a WebSocket session, throw an `IOException` rather than an `IllegalStateExcpetion` as required by `Writer` and strongly suggested by `OutputStream`. (markt) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 27: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update the internal fork of Commons Pool to 2.13.1. (markt) 
*   ![Image 28: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update the internal fork of Commons DBCP to 2.14.0. (markt) 
*   ![Image 29: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update Commons Daemon to 1.5.1. (markt) 
*   ![Image 30: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update ByteBuddy to 1.18.3. (markt) 
*   ![Image 31: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update UnboundID to 7.0.4. (markt) 
*   ![Image 32: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update Checkstyle to 12.3.1. (markt) 
*   ![Image 33: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to French translations. (markt) 
*   ![Image 34: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Japanese translations provided by tak7iji. (markt) 
*   ![Image 35: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Chinese translations provided by Yang. vincent.h and yong hu. (markt) 
*   ![Image 36: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update Tomcat Native to 2.0.12. (markt) 
*   ![Image 37: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add property "gpg.sign.files" to optionally disable release artefact signing with GPG. (rjung) 

### 2025-12-08 Tomcat 10.1.50 (schultz)

#### General

*   ![Image 38: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add `test.silent` property to suppress JUnit console output during test execution. Useful for cleaner console output when running tests with multiple threads. (csutherl) 

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 39: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69871](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69871): Increase log level to INFO for missing configuration for the rewrite valve. (remm) 
*   ![Image 40: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Add log warnings for additional Host `appBase` suspicious values. (remm) 
*   ![Image 41: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Remove hard dependency on tomcat-jni.jar for catalina.jar. `org.apache.catalina.Connector` no longer requires `org.apache.tomcat.jni.AprStatus` to be present. (markt) 
*   ![Image 42: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add the ability to use a custom function to generate the client identifier in the `CrawlerSessionManagerValve`. This is only available programmatically. Pull request [#902](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/902) by Brian Matzon. (markt) 
*   ![Image 43: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Change the SSO reauthentication behaviour for SPNEGO authentication so that a normal SPNEGO authentication is performed if the SSL Valve is configured with reauthentication enabled. This is so that the delegated credentials will be available to the web application. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 44: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Don't log an incorrect certificate `KeyStore` location when creating a TLS connector if the `KeyStore` instance has been set directly on the connector. (markt) 
*   ![Image 45: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) HTTP/0.9 only allows GET as the HTTP method. (remm) 
*   ![Image 46: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add `strictSni` attribute on the `Connector` to allow matching the `SSLHostConfig` configuration associated with the SNI host name to the `SSLHostConfig` configuration matched from the HTTP protocol host name. Non matching configurations will cause the request to be rejected. The attribute default value is `true`, enabling the matching. (remm) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 47: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69877](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69877): Catch IllegalArgumentException when processing URIs when creating the classpath to handle invalid URIs. (remm) 
*   ![Image 48: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix populating the classpath with the webapp classloader repositories. (remm) 

#### Clustering

*   ![Image 49: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a regression introduced in 10.1.45 that broke some clustering configurations. (markt) 

#### Web Applications

*   ![Image 50: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Manager: Fix abrupt truncation of the HTML and JSON complete server status output if one or more of the web applications failed to start. (schultz) 
*   ![Image 51: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Manager: Include web application state in the HTML and JSON complete server status output. (markt) 
*   ![Image 52: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Documentation: Expand the documentation to better explain when OCSP is supported and when it is not. (markt) 

#### jdbc-pool

*   ![Image 53: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[64083](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=64083): If the underlying connection has been closed, don't add it to the pool when it is returned. Pull request [#235](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/235) by Alex Panchenko. (markt) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 54: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add test profile system for selective test execution. Profiles can be specified via `-Dtest.profile=<name>` to run specific test subsets without using patterns directly. Profile patterns are defined in `test-profiles.properties`. (csutherl) 
*   ![Image 55: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update file extension to media type mappings to align with the current list used by the Apache Web Server (httpd). (markt) 
*   ![Image 56: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update the packaged version of the Tomcat Migration Tool for Jakarta EE to 1.0.10. (markt) 
*   ![Image 57: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update Commons Daemon to 1.5.0. (markt) 
*   ![Image 58: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update Byte Buddy to 1.18.2. (markt) 
*   ![Image 59: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update Checkstyle to 12.2.0. (markt) 
*   ![Image 60: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Spanish translations provided by White Vogel. (markt) 
*   ![Image 61: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to French translations. (remm) 
*   ![Image 62: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Japanese translations provided by tak7iji. (markt) 

### 2025-11-10 Tomcat 10.1.49 (schultz)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 63: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) When generating the class path in the Loader, re-order the check on individual class path components to avoid a potential `NullPointerException`. Identified by Coverity Scan. (markt) 
*   ![Image 64: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix SSL socket factory configuration in the JNDI realm. Based on pull request [#915](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/915) by Joshua Rogers. (remm) 
*   ![Image 65: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Add an attribute, `digestInRfc3112Order`, to `MessageDigestCredentialHandler` to control the order in which the credential and salt are digested. By default, the current, non-RFC 3112 compliant, order of salt then credential will be used. This default will change in Tomcat 12 to the RFC 3112 compliant order of credential then salt. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 66: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Graceful failure for OCSP on BoringSSL in the FFM code. (remm) 
*   ![Image 67: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix use of `deferAccept` attribute in JMX, since it is normally only removed in Tomcat 11. (remm) 
*   ![Image 68: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69866](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69866): Fix a memory leak when using a trust store with the OpenSSL provider. Pull request [#912](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/912) by aogburn. (markt) 
*   ![Image 69: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix potential crash on shutdown when a Connector depends on the Tomcat Native library. (markt) 
*   ![Image 70: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix AJP message length check. Pull request [#916](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/916) by Joshua Rogers. (remm) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 71: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69862](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69862): Avoid NPE unwrapping Servlet exception which would hide some exception details. Patch submitted by Eric Blanquer. (remm) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 72: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update the internal fork of Apache Commons BCEL to 6.11.0. (markt) 
*   ![Image 73: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update to Byte Buddy 1.17.8. (markt) 
*   ![Image 74: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update to Checkstyle 12.1.1. (markt) 
*   ![Image 75: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update to Jacoco 0.8.14. (markt) 
*   ![Image 76: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update to SpotBugs 4.9.8. (markt) 
*   ![Image 77: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update to JSign 7.4. (markt) 
*   ![Image 78: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update Maven Resolver Ant Tasks to 1.6.0. (rjung) 
*   ![Image 79: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to French translations. (remm) 
*   ![Image 80: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Japanese translations provided by tak7iji. (markt) 

### 2025-10-13 Tomcat 10.1.48 (schultz)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 81: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Log warnings when the SSO configuration does not comply with the documentation. (remm) 
*   ![Image 82: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Deprecate the `RemoteAddrFilter` and `RemoteAddrValve` in favour of the `RemoteCIDRFilter` and `RemoteCIDRValve`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 83: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69837](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69837): Fix corruption of the class path generated by the Loader when running on Windows. (markt) 
*   ![Image 84: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Reject requests that map to invalid Windows file names earlier. (markt) 
*   ![Image 85: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69839](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69839): Ensure that changes to session IDs (typically after authentication) are promulgated to the SSO Valve to ensure that SSO entries are fully clean-up on session expiration. Patch provided by Kim Johan Andersson. (markt) 
*   ![Image 86: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a race condition in the creation of the storage location for the `FileStore`. (markt) 

#### Coyote

### 2025-04-08 Tomcat 10.1.40 (schultz)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 197: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Return 400 if the amount of content sent for a partial PUT is inconsistent with the range that was specified. (remm) 
*   ![Image 198: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add a new `RateLimiter` implementation, `org.apache.catalina.util.ExactRateLimiter`, that can be used with `org.apache.catalina.filters.RateLimitFilter` to provide rate limit based on the exact values configured. Based on pull request [#794](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/794) by Chenjp. (markt) 
*   ![Image 199: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix parsing of the `time-taken` token in the `ExtendedAccessLogValve`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 200: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix invocation of the FFM OpenSSL code for setting a SSL engine and FIPS mode. (remm) 
*   ![Image 201: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69600](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69600): Add IPv6 local addresses (RFC 4193 and RFC 4291) to the default internal proxies for the RemoteIpFilter and RemoteIpValve. (markt) 
*   ![Image 202: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69615](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69615): Improve integration with the not found class resources cache for users who are using a custom web application class loader and/or using reflection to dynamically add external repositories to the web application class loader. (markt) 
*   ![Image 203: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add a new initialisation parameter to the Default servlet - `allowPostAsGet` - which controls whether a direct request (i.e. not a forward or an include) for a static resource using the POST method will be processed as if the GET method had been used. If not allowed, the request will be rejected. The default behaviour of processing the request as if the GET method had been used is unchanged. (markt) 
*   ![Image 204: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69623](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69623): Correct a long standing regression that meant that calls to `ClassLoader.getResource().getContent()` failed when made from within a web application with resource caching enabled. (markt) 
*   ![Image 205: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69634](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69634): Avoid NPE on `JsonErrorReportValve`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 206: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Add missing `throwable` stack trace to `JsonErrorReportValve` equivalent to the one from `ErrorReportValve`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 207: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve the handling of `%nn` URL encoding in the RewriteValve and document how `%nn` URL encoding may be used with rewrite rules. (markt) 
*   ![Image 208: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a potential exception when calling `WebappClassLoaderBase.getResource("")`. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 210: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69614](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69614): HTTP/2 priority frames with an invalid priority field value should be ignored. (markt)

If used with an Eclipse JDT compiler version that does not support these values, a warning will be logged and the default will be used. (markt)

### 2025-03-07 Tomcat 10.1.39 (schultz)

### not released Tomcat 10.1.38 (schultz)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 227: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69602](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69602): Fix regression in releases from 12-2024 that were too strict and rejected weak etags in the `If-Range` header with a 400 response. Instead will consider it as a failed match since strong etags are required for `If-Range`. (remm) 

### not released Tomcat 10.1.37 (schultz)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 228: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) When looking up class loader resources by resource name, the resource name should not start with '/'. If the resource name does start with '/', Tomcat is lenient and looks it up as if the '/' was not present. When the web application class loader was configured with external repositories and names starting with '/' were used for lookups, it was possible that cached 'not found' results could effectively hide lookup results using the correct resource name. (markt) 
*   ![Image 229: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Enable the JNDIRealm to validate credentials provided to `HttpServletRequest.login(String username, String password)` when the realm is configured to use GSSAPI authentication. (markt) 
*   ![Image 230: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a bug in the JRE compatibility detection that incorrectly identified Java 19 and Java 20 as supporting Java 21 features. (markt) 
*   ![Image 231: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve the checks for exposure to and protection against CVE-2024-56337 so that reflection is not used unless required. The checks for whether the file system is case sensitive or not have been removed. (markt) 
*   ![Image 232: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for logging the connection ID (as returned by `ServletRequest.getServletConnection().getConnectionId()`) with the `AccessLogValve` and `ExtendedAccessLogValve`. Based on pull request [#814](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/814) by Dmole. (markt) 
*   ![Image 233: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid scenarios where temporary files used for partial PUT would not be deleted. (remm) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 234: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69575](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69575): Avoid using compression if a response is already compressed using `compress`, `deflate` or `zstd`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 235: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Use `Transfer-Encoding` for compression rather than `Content-Encoding` if the client submits a `TE` header containing `gzip`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 236: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a race condition in the handling of HTTP/2 stream reset that could cause unexpected 500 responses. (markt) 

#### Cluster

*   ![Image 237: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif)[69598](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69598): Add detection of service account token changes to the `KubernetesMembershipProvider` implementation and reload the token if it changes. Based on a patch by Miroslav Jezbera. (markt)

(markt)

The ETag generated will be a SHA-1 checksum of the resource content. (remm) 
*   ![Image 297: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Use client locale for directory listings. (remm) 
*   ![Image 298: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69439](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69439): Improve the handling of multiple `Cache-Control` headers in the `ExpiresFilter`. Based on pull request [#777](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/777) by Chenjp. (markt) 
*   ![Image 299: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69447](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69447): Update the support for caching classes the web application class loader cannot find to take account of classes loaded from external repositories. Prior to this fix, these classes could be incorrectly marked as not found. (markt) 
*   ![Image 300: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69466](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69466): Rework handling of HEAD requests. Headers explicitly set by users will not be removed and any header present in a HEAD request will also be present in the equivalent GET request. There may be some headers, as per RFC 9110, section 9.3.2, that are present in a GET request that are not present in the equivalent HEAD request. (markt) 
*   ![Image 301: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69471](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69471): Log instances of `CloseNowException` caught by `ApplicationDispatcher.invoke()` at debug level rather than error level as they are very likely to have been caused by a client disconnection or similar I/O issue. (markt) 
*   ![Image 302: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add a test case for the fix for [69442](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69442). Also refactor references to `application/x-www-form-urlencoded`. Based on pull request [#779](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/779) by Chenjp. (markt) 
*   ![Image 303: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69476](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69476): Catch possible ISE when trying to report PUT failure in the `DefaultServlet`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 304: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for [RateLimit header fields for HTTP (draft)](https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/draft-ietf-httpapi-ratelimit-headers) in the `RateLimitFilter`. Based on pull request [#775](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/775) provided by Chenjp. (markt) 
*   ![Image 305: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif)[#787](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/787): Add regression tests for [69478](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69478). Pull request provided by Thomas Krisch. (markt) 
*   ![Image 306: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) The default servlet now rejects HTTP range requests when two or more of the requested ranges overlap. Based on pull request [#782](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/782) provided by Chenjp. (markt) 
*   ![Image 307: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Enhance Content-Range verification for partial PUT requests handled by the default servlet. Provided by Chenjp in pull request [#778](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/778). (markt) 
*   ![Image 308: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Harmonize `DataSourceStore` lookup in the global resources to optionally avoid the `comp/env` prefix which is usually not used there. (remm) 
*   ![Image 309: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) As required by RFC 9110, the HTTP `Range` header will now only be processed for `GET` requests. Based on pull request [#790](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/790) provided by Chenjp. (markt) 
*   ![Image 310: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Deprecate the `useAcceptRanges` initialisation parameter for the default servlet. It will be removed in Tomcat 12 onwards where it will effectively be hard coded to `true`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 311: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add `DataSource` based property storage for the `WebdavServlet`. (remm) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 312: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Align `encodedSolidusHandling` with the Servlet specification. If the pass-through mode is used, any `%25` sequences will now also be passed through to avoid errors and/or corruption when the application decodes the path. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 313: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Follow-up to the fix for [69381](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69381). Apply the optimisation for method lookup performance in expression language to an additional location. (markt) 

#### Web applications

### not released Tomcat 10.1.32 (schultz)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 333: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for the new Servlet API method `HttpServletResponse.sendEarlyHints()`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 334: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif)55470: Add debug logging that reports the class path when a `ClassNotFoundException` occurs in the digester or the web application class loader. Based on a patch by Ralf Hauser. (markt) 
*   ![Image 335: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif)[69374](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69374): Properly separate between table header and body in `DefaultServlet`'s listing. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 336: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif)[69373](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69373): Make `DefaultServlet`'s HTML listing file last modified rendering better (flexible). (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 337: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Improve HTML output of `DefaultServlet`. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 338: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor `RateLimitFilter` to use `FilterBase` as the base class. The primary advantage for doing this is less code to process `init-param` values. (markt) 
*   ![Image 339: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif)[69370](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69370): `DefaultServlet`'s HTML listing uses incorrect labels. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 340: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid NPE in `CrawlerSessionManagerValve` for partially mapped requests. (remm) 
*   ![Image 341: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Add missing WebDAV `Lock-Token` header in the response when locking a folder. (remm) 
*   ![Image 342: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Invalid WebDAV lock requests should be rejected with 400. (remm) 
*   ![Image 343: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix regression in WebDAV when attempting to unlock a collection. (remm) 
*   ![Image 344: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Verify that destination is not locked for a WebDAV copy operation. (remm) 
*   ![Image 345: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Send 415 response to WebDAV `MKCOL` operations that include a request body since this is optional and unsupported. (remm) 
*   ![Image 346: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Enforce `DAV:` namespace on WebDAV XML elements. (remm) 
*   ![Image 347: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Do not allow a new WebDAV lock on a child resource if a parent collection is locked (RFC 4918 section 6.1). (remm) 
*   ![Image 348: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) WebDAV `DELETE` should remove any existing lock on successfully deleted resources. (remm) 
*   ![Image 349: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Remove WebDAV lock null support in accordance with RFC 4918 section 7.3 and annex D. Instead a lock on a non existing resource will create an empty file locked with a regular lock. (remm) 
*   ![Image 350: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Rewrite implementation of WebDAV shared locks to comply with RFC 4918. (remm) 
*   ![Image 351: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Implement WebDAV `If` header using code from the Apache Jackrabbit project. (remm) 
*   ![Image 352: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add `PropertyStore` interface in the WebDAV Servlet, to allow implementation of dead properties storage. The store used can be configured using the `propertyStore` init parameter of the WebDAV servlet by specifying the class name of the store. A simple non persistent implementation is used if no custom store is configured. (remm) 
*   ![Image 353: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Implement WebDAV `PROPPATCH` method using the newly added `PropertyStore`, and update `PROPFIND` to support it. (remm) 
*   ![Image 354: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Cache not found results when searching for web application class loader resources. This addresses performance problems caused by components such as `java.sql.DriverManager` which, in some circumstances, will search for the same class repeatedly. In a large web application this can cause performance problems. The size of the cache can be controlled via the new `notFoundClassResourceCacheSize` on the StandardContext. (markt) 
*   ![Image 355: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Stop after `INITIALIZED` state should be a noop since it is possible for subcomponents to be in `FAILED` after init. (remm) 
*   ![Image 356: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix incorrect web resource cache size calculations when there are concurrent `PUT` and `DELETE` requests for the same resource. (markt) 
*   ![Image 357: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add debug logging for the web resource cache so the current size can be tracked as resources are added and removed. (markt) 
*   ![Image 358: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Replace legacy WebDAV `opaquelocktoken:` scheme for lock tokens with `urn:uuid:` as recommended by RFC 4918, and remove `secret` init parameter. (remm) 
*   ![Image 359: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Concurrent reads and writes (e.g. `GET` and `PUT` / `DELETE`) for the same path caused corruption of the `FileResource` where some of the fields were set as if the file exists and some were set as if it does not. This resulted in inconsistent metadata. (markt) 
*   ![Image 360: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69415](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69415): Ensure that the `ExpiresFilter` only sets cache headers on `GET` and `HEAD` requests. Also skip requests where the application has set 
```
Cache-Control:
        no-store
```
. (markt) 
*   ![Image 361: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69419](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69419): Improve the performance of `ServletRequest.getAttribute()` when there are multiple levels of nested includes. Based on a patch provided by John Engebretson. (markt) 
*   ![Image 362: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) All applications to send an early hints informational response by calling `HttpServletResponse.sendError()` with a status code of 103. (schultz) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 363: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Return null SSL session id on zero length byte array returned from the SSL implementation. (remm) 
*   ![Image 364: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Skip OpenSSLConf with BoringSSL since it is unsupported. (remm) 
*   ![Image 365: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Create the `HttpParser` in `Http11Processor` if it is not present on the `AbstractHttp11Protocol` to provide better lifecycle robustness for regular HTTP/1.1. The new behavior was introduced on a previous refactoring to improve HTTP/2 performance. (remm) 
*   ![Image 366: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)`OpenSSLContext` will now throw a `KeyManagementException` if something is known to have gone wrong in the `init` method, which is the behavior documented by `javax.net.ssl.SSLContext.init`. This makes error handling more consistent. (remm) 
*   ![Image 367: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69379](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69379): The default HEAD response no longer includes the payload HTTP header fields as per section 9.3.2 of RFC 9110. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 368: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Add back tag release method as deprecated in the runtime for compat with old generated code. (remm) 
*   ![Image 369: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69399](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69399): Fix regression caused by the improvement [69333](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69333) which caused the tag `release` to be called when using tag pooling, and to be skipped when not using it. Patch submitted by Michal Sobkiewicz. (remm) 
*   ![Image 370: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69381](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69381): Improve method lookup performance in expression language. When the required method has no arguments there is no need to consider casting or coercion and the method lookup process can be simplified. Based on pull request [#770](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/770) by John Engebretson. (markt) 
*   ![Image 371: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69382](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69382): Improve the performance of the JSP include action by re-using results of relatively expensive method calls in the generated code rather than repeating them. Patch provided by John Engebretson. (markt) 
*   ![Image 372: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69398](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69398): Avoid unnecessary object allocation in `PageContextImpl`. Based on a suggestion by John Engebretson. (markt) 
*   ![Image 373: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69406](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69406): When using `StringInterpreterEnum`, do not throw an `IllegalArgumentException` when an invalid `Enum` is encountered. Instead, resolve the value at runtime. Patch provided by John Engebretson. (markt) 
*   ![Image 374: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69429](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69429): Optimise EL evaluation of method parameters for methods that do not accept any parameters. Patch provided by John Engebretson. (markt) 
*   ![Image 375: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Further optimise EL evaluation of method parameters. Patch provided by Paolo B. (markt)

*   ![Image 394: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69316](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69316): Ensure that `FastHttpDateFormat#getCurrentDate()` (used to generate Date headers for HTTP responses) generates the correct string for the given input. Prior to this change, the output may have wrong by one second in some cases. Pull request [#751](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/751) provided by Chenjp. (markt)

Trailer fields no longer need to be recieved before the headers of the subsequent stream nor are trailer fields for an in progress stream swallowed if the Connector is paused before the trailer fields are received. (markt)

This could lead to incorrect processing times appearing in the access log. (markt)

### 2024-09-10 Tomcat 10.1.29 (schultz)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 410: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve performance of `ApplicationHttpRequest.parseParameters()`. Based on sample code and test cases provided by John Engebretson. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 411: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a regression in the fix for non-blocking reads of chunked request bodies that caused `InputStream.available()` to return a non-zero value when there was no data to read. In some circumstances this could cause a blocking read to block waiting for more data rather than return the data it had already received. (markt) 
*   ![Image 412: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add a new attribute `cookiesWithoutEquals` to the `Rfc6265CookieProcessor`. The default behaviour is unchanged. (markt) 
*   ![Image 413: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that Tomcat sends a TLS close_notify message after receiving one from the client when using the `OpenSSLImplementation`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 414: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69301](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69301): Fix trailer headers replacing non-trailer headers when writing response headers to the access log. Based on a patch and test case provided by hypnoce. (markt) 
*   ![Image 415: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69302](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69302): If an HTTP/2 client resets a stream before the request body is fully written, ensure that any `ReadListener` is notified via a call to `ReadListener.onErrror()`. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 416: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Switch the `TldScanner` back to logging detailed scan results at debug level rather than trace level. (markt) 

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 417: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) If a blocking message write exceeds the timeout, don't attempt the write again before throwing the exception. (markt) 
*   ![Image 418: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) An EncodeException being thrown during a message write should not automatically cause the connection to close. The application should handle the exception and make the decision whether or not to close the connection. (markt) 

#### Web applications

*   ![Image 419: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Documentation. Align the logging configuration documentation with the current defaults. (markt) 

#### jdbc-pool

*   ![Image 420: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69255](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69255): Correct a regression in the fix for [69206](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69206) that meant exceptions executing statements were wrapped in an `java.lang.reflect.UndeclaredThrowableException` rather than the application seeing the original `SQLException`. Fixed by pull request [#744](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/744) provided by Michael Clarke. (markt) 
*   ![Image 421: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69279](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69279): Correct a regression in the fix for [69206](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69206) that meant that methods that previously returned a `null``ResultSet` were returning a proxy with a null delegate. Fixed by pull request [#745](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/745) provided by Huub de Beer. (markt) 

#### Other

### not released Tomcat 10.1.27 (schultz)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 433: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for RFC 8297 (Early Hints). Applications can use this feature by casting the `HttpServletResponse` to `org.apache.catalina.connector.Reponse` and then calling the method `void sendEarlyHints()`. This method will be added to the Servlet API (removing the need for the cast) in Servlet 6.2 onwards. (markt) 
*   ![Image 434: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69214](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69214): Do not reject a CORS request that uses POST but does not include a `content-type` header. Tomcat now correctly processes this as a simple CORS request. Based on a patch suggested by thebluemountain. (markt) 
*   ![Image 435: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Refactor `SpnegoAuthenticator` so it uses `Subject.callAs()` rather than `Subject.doAs()` when the available. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 436: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that HTTP/2 stream input buffers are only created when there is a request body to be read. (markt) 
*   ![Image 437: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor creation of HttpParser instances from the Processor level to the Protocol level since the parser configuration depends on the protocol and the parser is, otherwise, stateless. (markt) 
*   ![Image 438: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Align HTTP/2 with HTTP/1.1 and recycle the container internal request and response processing objects by default. This behaviour can be controlled via the new `discardRequestsAndResponses` attribute on the HTTP/2 upgrade protocol. (markt) 

#### jdbc-pool

*   ![Image 439: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[69206](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69206): Ensure statements returned from `Statement` methods `executeQuery()`, `getResultSet()` and `getGeneratedKeys()` are correctly wrapped before being returned to the caller. Based on pull request [#742](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/742) provided by Michael Clarke. 

#### Other

*   ![Image 440: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix packaging regression with missing osgi information following addition of the `test-only` build target. (remm)

*   ![Image 507: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Reduce the time spent waiting for the connector to unlock. The previous default of 10s was noticeably too long for cases where the unlock has failed. The wait time is now 100ms plus twice `socket.unlockTimeout`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 508: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that the `onAllDataRead()` event is triggered when the request body uses chunked encoding and is read using non-blocking IO. (markt)

### 2024-04-23 Tomcat 10.1.23 (schultz)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 530: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Deprecate and remove `sessionCounter` (replaced by the addition of the active session count and the expired session count, as a reasonable approximation) and `duplicates` (which does not represent a possible event in current implementations) statistics from the session manager. (remm) 
*   ![Image 531: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[68890](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68890) Align output encoding of JSPs in the Manager webapp with the XML declarations in those same files. (schultz) 
*   ![Image 532: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Update Basic authentication to implement the requirements of RFC 7617 including the changing of the `trimCredentials` setting which is now defaults to `false`. Note that the `trimCredentials` setting will be removed in Tomcat 11. (markt) 

#### Coyote

### 2024-03-25 Tomcat 10.1.20 (schultz)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 546: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Minor performance improvement for building filter chains. Based on ideas from pull request [#702](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/702) by Luke Miao. (remm) 
*   ![Image 547: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Align error handling for `Writer` and `OutputStream`. Ensure use of either once the response has been recycled triggers a `NullPointerException` provided that `discardFacades` is configured with the default value of `true`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 548: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[68692](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68692): The standard thread pool implementations that are configured using the `Executor` element now implement `ExecutorService` for better support NIO2. (remm) 
*   ![Image 549: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[68495](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68495): When restoring a saved POST request after a successful FORM authentication, ensure that neither the URI, the query string nor the protocol are corrupted when restoring the request body. (markt) 
*   ![Image 550: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) After forwarding a request, attempt to unwrap the response in order to suspend it, instead of simply closing it if it was wrapped. Add a new `suspendWrappedResponseAfterForward` boolean attribute on `Context` to control the bahavior, defaulting to `false`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 551: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[68721](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68721): Workaround a possible cause of duplicate class definitions when using `ClassFileTransformer`s and the transformation of a class also triggers the loading of the same class. (markt) 
*   ![Image 552: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) The rewrite valve should not do a rewrite if the output is identical to the input. (remm) 
*   ![Image 553: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Add a new `valveSkip` (or `VS`) rule flag to the rewrite valve to allow skipping over the next valve in the Catalina pipeline. (remm) 
*   ![Image 554: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Add `highConcurrencyStatus` attribute to the `SemaphoreValve` to optionally allow the valve to return an error status code to the client when a permit cannot be acquired from the semaphore. (remm) 
*   ![Image 555: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add checking of the "age" of the running Tomcat instance since its build-date to the SecurityListener, and log a warning if the server is old. (schultz) 
*   ![Image 556: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) When using the `AsyncContext`, throw an `IllegalStateException`, rather than allowing an `NullPointerException`, if an attempt is made to use the `AsyncContext` after it has been recycled. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 557: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve the HTTP/2 stream prioritisation process. If a stream uses all of the connection windows and still has content to write, it will now be added to the backlog immediately rather than waiting until the write attempt for the remaining content. (markt) 
*   ![Image 558: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Add `threadsMaxIdleTime` attribute to the endpoint, to allow configuring the amount of time before an internal executor will scale back to the configured `minSpareThreads` size. (remm) 
*   ![Image 559: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a regression in the support for user provided `SSLContext` instances that broke the `org.apache.catalina.security.TLSCertificateReloadListener`. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 560: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for specifying Java 22 (with the value `22`) as the compiler source and/or compiler target for JSP compilation. If used with an Eclipse JDT compiler version that does not support these values, a warning will be logged and the default will used. (markt) 
*   ![Image 561: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Handle the case where the JSP engine forwards a request/response to a Servlet that uses an `OutputStream` rather than a `Writer`. This was triggering an `IllegalStateException` on code paths where there was a subsequent attempt to obtain a `Writer`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 562: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Correctly handle the case where a tag library is packaged in a JAR file and the web application is deployed as a WAR file rather than an unpacked directory. (markt) 
*   ![Image 563: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Prevent the web application's ClassLoader from being pinned by the JSP compiler if an application uses a custom XMLInputFactory. Based upon a suggestion from Simon Niederberger. (schultz) 

#### Cluster

*   ![Image 564: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid updating request count stats on async. (remm) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 565: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to French translations. (remm) 
*   ![Image 566: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Japanese translations by tak7iji. (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 569: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct JPMS and OSGi meta-data for `tomcat-embed-core.jar` by removing reference to `org.apache.catalina.ssi` package that is no longer included in the JAR. Based on pull request [#684](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/684) by Jendrik Johannes. (markt)

*   ![Image 573: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[68089](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68089): Further improve the performance of request attribute access for `ApplicationHttpRequest` and `ApplicationRequest`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 574: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[68559](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68559): Allow asynchronous error handling to write to the response after an error during asynchronous processing. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 575: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Setting a `null` value for a cookie attribute should remove the attribute. (markt) 
*   ![Image 576: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Make asynchronous error handling more robust. Ensure that once a connection is marked to be closed, further asynchronous processing cannot change that. (markt) 
*   ![Image 577: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Make asynchronous error handling more robust. Ensure that once the call to `AsyncListener.onError()` has returned to the container, only container threads can access the `AsyncContext`. This protects against various race conditions that would otherwise occur if application threads continued to access the `AsyncContext`. 
*   ![Image 578: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Review usage of debug logging and downgrade trace or data dumping operations from debug level to trace. In particular, most of the HTTP/2 debug logging has been changed to trace level. (remm) 
*   ![Image 579: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Add support for user provided `SSLContext` instances configured on `SSLHostConfigCertificate` instances. Based on pull request [#673](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/673) provided by Hakan Altındağ. (markt) 
*   ![Image 580: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Partial fix for [68558](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68558): Cache the result of converting to `String` for request URI, HTTP header names and the request `Content-Type` value to improve performance by reducing repeated `byte[]` to `String` conversions. (markt) 
*   ![Image 581: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve error reporting to HTTP/2 clients for header processing errors by reporting problems at the end of the frame where the error was detected rather than at the end of the headers. (markt) 
*   ![Image 582: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Remove the remaining reference to a stream once the stream has been recycled. This makes the stream eligible for garbage collection earlier and thereby improves scalability. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 583: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[68546](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68546): Generate optimal size and types for JSP imports maps, as suggested by John Engebretson. (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 740: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66567](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66567): Fix missing `IllegalArgumentException` after the Tomcat code was converted to using URI instead of URL. (remm) 
*   ![Image 741: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Escape timestamp output in `AccessLogValve` if a `SimpleDateFormat` is used which contains verbatim characters that need escaping. (rjung) 
*   ![Image 742: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Change output of vertical tab in `AccessLogValve` from `\v` to `\u000b`. (rjung) 
*   ![Image 743: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Improve performance of escaping in `AccessLogValve` roughly by a factor of two. (rjung) 
*   ![Image 744: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Improve `JsonAccessLogValve`: support more patterns like for headers and attributes. Those will be logged as sub objects. (rjung) 
*   ![Image 745: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[#613](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/613): Fix possible partial corrupted file copies when using file locking protection or the manager servlet. Submitted by Jack Shirazi. (remm) 
*   ![Image 746: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add RateLimitFilter which can be used to mitigate DoS and Brute Force attacks. (isapir) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 747: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for a new character set, `gb18030-2022` - introduced in Java 21, to the character set caching mechanism. (markt) 
*   ![Image 748: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix an edge case in HTTP header parsing and ensure that HTTP headers without names are treated as invalid. (markt) 
*   ![Image 749: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Deprecate the HTTP Connector settings `rejectIllegalHeader` and `allowHostHeaderMismatch` as they have been removed in Tomcat 11 onwards. (markt) 
*   ![Image 750: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66591](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66591): Fix a regression introduced in the fix for [66512](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66512) that meant that an AJP Send Headers was not sent for responses where no HTTP headers were set. (markt) 

#### Jasper

#### WebSocket

(markt) 
*   ![Image 753: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66575](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66575): Avoid unchecked use of the backing array of a buffer provided by the user in the compression transformation. (remm)

### 2023-04-19 Tomcat 10.1.8 (schultz)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 761: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65995](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65995): Implement RFC 9239 and use `text/javascript` as the media type for JavaScript rather than `application/javascript`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 762: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add an access log valve that uses a json format. Based on pull request [#539](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/539) provided by Thomas Meyer. (remm) 
*   ![Image 763: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Harden the FORM authentication process against DoS attacks by using a reduced session timeout if the FORM authentication process creates a session. The duration of this timeout is configured by the `authenticationSessionTimeout` attribute of the FORM authenticator. (markt) 
*   ![Image 764: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66527](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66527): Correct the Javadoc for the `Tomcat.addWebapp()` methods that incorrectly stated that the `docBase` parameter could be a relative path. (markt) 
*   ![Image 765: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66524](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66524) Correct eviction ordering in WebResource cache to be LRU as intended. (schultz) 
*   ![Image 766: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Use server.xml to reduce the default value of `maxParameterCount` from 10,000 to 1,000. If not configured in server.xml, the default remains 10,000. (markt) 
*   ![Image 767: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Update Digest authentication support to align with RFC 7616. This adds a new configuration attribute, `algorithms`, to the `DigestAuthenticator` with a default of `SHA-256,MD5`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 768: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Add support code for custom user attributes in `RealmBase`. Based on code from [#473](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/473) by Carsten Klein. (remm) 
*   ![Image 769: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Expand the set of HTTP request headers considered sensitive that should be skipped when generating a response to a `TRACE` request. This aligns with 11.0.x. (markt) 
*   ![Image 770: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66541](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66541): Improve handling for cached resources for resources that use custom URL schemes. The scheme specific `equals()` and `hashCode()` algorithms, if present, will now be used for URLs for these resources. This addresses a potential performance issue with some OSGi custom URL schemes that can trigger potentially slow DNS lookups in some configurations. Based on a patch provided by Tom Whitmore. (markt) 
*   ![Image 771: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) When using a custom session manager deployed as part of the web application, avoid `ClassNotFoundException`s when validating session IDs extracted from requests. (markt) 
*   ![Image 772: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66543](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66543): Give `StandardContext#fireRequestDestroyEvent` its own log message. (fschumacher) 
*   ![Image 773: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66554](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66554): Initialize Random during server initialization to avoid possible JVM thread creation in the webapp context on some platforms. (remm) 
*   ![Image 774: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Make the server utility executor available to webapps using a Servlet context attribute named `org.apache.tomcat.util.threads.ScheduledThreadPoolExecutor`. (remm) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 775: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) JSON filter should support specific escaping for common special characters as defined in RFC 8259. Based on code submitted by Thomas Meyer. (remm) 
*   ![Image 776: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66511](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66511): Fix `GzipOutputFilter` (used for compressed HTTP responses) when used with direct buffers. Patch suggested by Arjen Poutsma. (markt) 
*   ![Image 777: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66512](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66512): Align AJP handling of invalid HTTP response headers (they are now removed from the response) with HTTP. (markt) 
*   ![Image 778: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66530](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66530): Correct a regression in the fix for bug [66442](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66442) that meant that streams without a response body did not decrement the active stream count when completing leading to `ERR_HTTP2_SERVER_REFUSED_STREAM` for some connections. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 779: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix bug that meant some instances of coercing a `LambdaExpression` to a functional interface invocation failed. (markt)

A new warning message will be logged if the file transfer is cancelled. (markt) 

#### WebSocket

The value is not decoded but it is checked for the correct length and that only valid characters from the base64 alphabet are used. (markt)

### 2023-01-13 Tomcat 10.1.5 (markt)

The regression broke lookups for resources that contained one or more characters in their name that required escaping when used in a URI path. (markt) 
*   ![Image 825: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66392](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66392): Change the default value of `AccessLogValve`'s file encoding to UTF-8 and update documentation. (lihan)

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 827: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) When resetting an HTTP/2 stream because the final response has been generated before the request has been fully read, use the HTTP/2 error code `NO_ERROR` so that client does not discard the response. Based on a suggestion by Lorenzo Dalla Vecchia. (markt) 
*   ![Image 828: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66385](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66385): Correct a bug in HTTP/2 where a non-blocking read for a new frame with the NIO2 connector was incorrectly made using the read timeout leading to unexpected stream closure. (markt) 
*   ![Image 830: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for specifying Java 21 (with the value `21`) as the compiler source and/or compiler target for JSP compilation. ### 2022-11-14 Tomcat 10.1.2 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 856: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif)[66209](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66209): Add a configuration option to allow bloom filters used to index JAR files to be retained for the lifetime of the web application. Prior to this addition, the indexes were always flushed by the periodic calls to `WebResourceRoot.gc()`. As part of this addition, configuration of archive indexing moves from `Context` to `WebResourceRoot`. Based on a patch provided by Rahul Jaisimha. (markt) 
*   ![Image 857: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66330](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66330): Correct a regression introduced when fixing [62897](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=62897) that meant any value configured for `skipMemoryLeakChecksOnJvmShutdown` on the `Context` was ignored and the default was always used. (markt) 
*   ![Image 858: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66331](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66331): Fix a regression in refactoring for `Stack` on the `SystemLogHandler` which caught incorrect exception. (lihan) 
*   ![Image 859: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66338](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66338): Fix a regression that caused a nuance in refactoring for `ErrorReportValve`. (lihan) 
*   ![Image 860: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Escape values used to construct output for the `JsonErrorReportValve` to ensure that it always outputs valid JSON. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 861: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct the date format used with the expires attribute of HTTP cookies. A single space rather than a single dash should be used to separate the day, month and year components to be compliant with RFC 6265. (markt) 
*   ![Image 862: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Include the name of the current stream state in the error message when a stream is cancelled due to an attempt to write to the stream when it is in a state that does not permit writes. (markt) 
*   ![Image 863: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) NIO writes never return -1 so refactor `CLOSED_NIO_CHANNEL` not to do so and remove checks for this return value. Based on [#562](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/562) by tianshuang. (markt) 
*   ![Image 864: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Remove unnecessary code that exposed the `asyncTimeout` to components that never used it. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 865: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66294](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66294): Make the use of a privileged block to obtain the thread context class loader added to address [62080](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=62080) optional and disabled by default. This is now controlled by the `org.apache.el.GET_CLASSLOADER_USE_PRIVILEGED` system property. (markt) 
*   ![Image 866: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66317](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66317): Fix for Lambda coercion security manager missing privileges. Based on pull request #557 by Isaac Rivera Rivas (lihan) 
*   ![Image 867: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66325](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66325): Fix concurrency issue in evaluation of expression language containing lambda expressions. (markt)

### 2022-07-20 Tomcat 10.1.0-M17 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 952: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66104](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66104): Avoid error message by not trying to clean up old files from the logging directory before the directory has been created. Based on [#521](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/521) by HanLi. (markt) 
*   ![Image 953: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update the Jakarta Common Annotations API to 2.1.1. This deprecates the `ManagedBean` annotation which will be removed in a future release. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 954: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Provide dedicated loggers (`org.apache.tomcat.util.net.NioEndpoint.handshake` / `org.apache.tomcat.util.net.Nio2Endpoint.handshake`) for TLS handshake failures. (markt) 
*   ![Image 955: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Enable the use of the FIPS provider for TLS enabled Connectors when using Tomcat Native 1.2.34 onwards built with OpenSSL 3.0.x onwards. (markt) 
*   ![Image 956: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Remove the `jvmRoute` system property used to configure a default value for the `jvmRoute` attribute of an Engine. (markt) 
*   ![Image 957: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update experimental Panama modules with support for OpenSSL 3.0+. OpenSSL 1.1 remains supported. (remm) 
*   ![Image 958: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a regression in the refactoring to support experimentation with project Loom that broke HTTP/2 support if async IO was disabled. (markt) 
*   ![Image 959: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix duplicate Poller registration with HTTP/2, NIO and async IO that could cause HTTP/2 connections to unexpectedly fail. (markt) 
*   ![Image 960: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Refactor Panama module to better take advantage of the Panama preview API updates and fixes. Improves memory session usage and avoids some allocations. Review from Maurizio Cimadamore. (remm) 
*   ![Image 961: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update the minimum recommended version of the Tomcat Native Library to 2.0.1. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 962: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for specifying Java 19 (with the value `19`) as the compiler source and/or compiler target for JSP compilation. If used with an Eclipse JDT compiler version that does not support these values, a warning will be logged and the default will used. (markt) 

#### WebSocket

(markt)

### 2022-06-09 Tomcat 10.1.0-M16 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 980: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Update the memory leak protection code to support stopping application created executor threads when running on Java 19 and later. (markt) 
*   ![Image 981: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve the error message if a required `--add-opens` option is missing. (markt) 
*   ![Image 982: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Disable the memory leak correction code enabled by the Context attribute `clearReferencesObjectStreamClassCaches` when running on a JRE that includes a fix for the underlying memory leak. (markt) 
*   ![Image 983: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[#515](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/515): Avoid deadlock on startup with some utility executor configurations. Submitted by Han Li. (remm) 
*   ![Image 984: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66068](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66068): Ensure that the changes made to a request by the `RemoteIPValve` persist after the request is put into asynchronous mode. (markt) 
*   ![Image 985: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Include the major version in the recommended version used for Tomcat Native with the `AprLifecycleListener`. (markt)

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 987: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Additional fix for [65118](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65118). Fix a potential `NullPointerException` when pruning closed HTTP/2 streams from the connection. (markt) 
*   ![Image 988: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor synchronization blocks locking on `SocketWrapper` to use `ReentrantLock` to support users wishing to experiment with project Loom. (markt) 
*   ![Image 989: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66076](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66076): When using TLS with non-blocking writes and the NIO connector, ensure that flushing the buffers attempts to empty all of the output buffers. (markt) 
*   ![Image 990: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66084](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66084): Correctly calculate bytes written to a response. Pull request [#516](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/516) provided by aooohan HanLi. (markt) 
*   ![Image 991: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Correct a regression in the support added for encrypted PKCS#1 formatted private keys in the previous release that broke support for unencrypted PKCS#1 formatted private keys. (jfclere/markt) 
*   ![Image 992: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Remove support for NPN when using the Tomcat Native Connector as NPN was never standardised and browser support for NPN was removed several years ago. (markt) 

#### Jasper

#### Tribes
