### 2022-05-16 Tomcat 10.1.0-M15 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1003: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif)[65853](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65853): Refactor the `CsrfPreventionFilter` to make it easier for sub-classes to modify the nonce generation and storage. Based on suggestions by Marvin Fröhlich. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1004: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65991](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65991): Avoid NPE with `SSLAuthenticator` when `boundOnInit` is used on a connector, during the check for client certificate authentication availability. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1005: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66009](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66009): Use `getSubjectX500Principal().toString()` rather than `getSubjectX500Principal().getName(...)` to retrieve a certificate DN, to match the output of the deprecated `getSubjectDN().getName()` that was used previously. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1006: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Revert the change in 10.1.0-M11 that added a mapping of `Shift_JIS` for the `ja` locale to the default mappings used by `ServletResponse.setLocale()` as it caused regressions for applications using UTF-8. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1007: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Provide a property source that sources values from Kubernetes service bindings. Pull request [#512](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/512) provided by Sumit Kulhadia and Gareth Evans. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1008: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif)[#501](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/501): Add new `maxHttpRequestHeaderSize` and `maxHttpResponseHeaderSize` attributes which allow setting the maximum HTTP header sizes independently. If not specified, the value of the `maxHttpHeaderSize` connector attribute will be used. Submitted by Zhongming Hua. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1009: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) The root cause of the Linux kernel duplicate accept bug has been identified along with the version of the kernel that includes the fix. The error message displayed when this bug occurs has been updated to reflect this new information and to advise users to update to a version of the OS that uses kernel 5.10 or later. Thanks to Christopher Gual for the research into this issue. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1010: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Remove the custom UTF-8 decoder that was introduced to work around various UTF-8 decoding bugs in Java. These issues were fixed in early Java 8 releases. Now the minimum Java version is 11, we can be sure that Tomcat will not be running on a JRE where these issues are present. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1011: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66023](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66023): Improve the fix for [65726](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65726) and support HTTP upgrade with a request body for a wider set of use cases. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1012: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66035](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66035): Add NULL check on the SSL session reference in the Panama code before accessing the session id and creation time. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1013: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for encrypted PKCS#1 formatted private keys when configuring the internal, in memory key store. Based on [#511](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/511). (jfclere/markt) 
*   ![Image 1014: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Remove the `prestartminSpareThreads` attribute of the `StandardThreadExecutor` since all core threads are always started by default making this attribute meaningless. Pull request [#510](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/510) provided by Aooohan. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 1015: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) To align with the JSP 3.1 specification, make the `jsp:plugin` action a NO-OP. No HTML will be generated as a result the `jsp:plugin` action being included in a JSP. This is be because the associated HTML elements are no longer supported by any major browser. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1016: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66031](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66031): Fix NPE when using a custom JspFactory. Patch by Jean-Louis Monteiro. (remm) 

#### Webapps

*   ![Image 1017: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[66008](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66008): In the documentation web application, clarify the recommendation for the use the `trimSpaces` option for Jasper in production environments. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1018: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Update the documentation web application to state that the `EncryptInterceptor` does not provide sufficient protection to run Tomcat clustering over an untrusted network. This is CVE-2022-29885. (markt) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 1019: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Chinese translations contributed by shawn. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1020: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to French translations. (remm)

*   ![Image 1023: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Korean translations. (woonsan)

This fixes a known regression in 1.3.0 when configuring the Windows service with custom scripts as described in [66055](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66055). (markt)

### 2022-04-01 Tomcat 10.1.0-M14 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1027: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65736](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65736): Disable the `forceString` option for the JNDI `BeanFactory` and replace it with an automatic search for an alternative setter with the same name that accepts a `String`. This is a security hardening measure. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1028: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Remove the `WebappClassLoaderBase.getResources()` method as it is not used and if something accidentally exposes the class loader this method can be used to gain access to Tomcat internals. (markt)

(markt) 
*   ![Image 1034: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif)[65975](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65975): Add a warning if a TLS virtual host is configured for TLS 1.3 with a JSSE implementation and a web application is configured for `CLIENT-CERT` authentication. `CLIENT-CERT` authentication requires post-handshake authentication (PHA) when used with TLS 1.3 but the JSSE TLS 1.3 implementation does not support PHA. (markt)

This typically happens when no ROOT context is defined. Pull request by elkman. (markt)

Test case code submitted by Istvan Szekely. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1060: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix potential thread-safety issue that could cause HTTP/1.1 request processing to wait, and potentially timeout, waiting for additional data when the full request has been received. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1061: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Throw `IOException` rather than `IllegalStateException` when the application attempts to write to an HTTP/2 stream after the client has closed the stream. (markt)

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 1117: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Remove the `ALLOW_UNSUPPORTED_EXTENSIONS` system property. As per RFC 6455, all extensions are optional. If an endpoint declares an extension that isn't supported there is no need to trigger an error. The extension can just be excluded from the result of the negotiation. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1118: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Remove the `DISABLE_BUILTIN_EXTENSIONS`. It was added to enable Tomcat to pass the WebSocket TCK but after updates to the TCK, it is no longer required. (markt)

### 2021-11-15 Tomcat 10.1.0-M7 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1154: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor `HttpServlet` so the default `doHead()` implementation now calls `doGet()` and relies on the container to ensure that the response body is not sent. The previous behaviour (wrapping the response) may be enabled per Servlet by setting the `jakarta.servlet.http.legacyDoHead` Servlet initialisation parameter to `true`. This aligns Tomcat with recent changes updates for Servlet 6.0 in the Jakarta Servlet specification project. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1155: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for setting generic attributes for session cookies. This aligns Apache Tomcat with recent changes in the Jakarta Servlet specification project. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1156: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Do not add a trailing `/` to a request URI during canonicalization. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1157: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Invalid byte sequences (typically in %nn form) in a request URi that are not valid for the given URI encoding now trigger a 400 response. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1158: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that a request URI starts with a `/`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1159: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add a new Connector option, `rejectSuspiciousURIs` that will causes 'suspicious' (see the Servlet 6.0 specification) URIs to be rejected with a 400 response. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1160: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve robustness of JNDIRealm for exceptions occurring when getting the connection. Also add missing close when running into issues getting the passord of a user. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1161: Docs: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/docs.gif) Add Javadoc comment which listeners must be nested within `Server` elements only. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 1162: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for custom caching strategies for web application resources. This initial implementation allows control over whether or not a resource is cached. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1163: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Improve performance of Connector shutdown - primarily to reduce the time it takes to run the test suite. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1164: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif)[#457](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/457): Add a `toString()` method to `MimeHeader` to aid debugging. (dblevins) 
*   ![Image 1165: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add experimental OpenSSL support through the Panama API incubating in Java 17, with support for OpenSSL 1.1+. This no longer requires tomcat-native or APR. Please refer to the `openssl-java17` module for more details. (remm) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 1166: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Regenerate the EL parser using JavaCC 7.0.10. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1167: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a bug that prevented the EL parser correctly parsing a literal Map that used variables rather than literals for both keys and values. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1168: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Ensure that the `getType()` method of any `ELResolver` implementation returns `null` if either the `ELResolver` or the resolved property is read-only to align Tomcat with recent updates in the Jakarta EL specification project. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1169: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Implement an alternative solution to support the JSP page directive attribute `isThreadSafe` now that the `SingleThreadModel` interface has been removed from the Servlet API. The new approach synchronizes the `service()` method. 

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 1170: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Add a new method
```
ServerEndpointConfig.Configurator.getContainerDefaultConfigurator()
```
to align with recent updates in the WebSocket specification project. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1171: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Add a new method `ServerContainer.upgradeHttpToWebSocket()` to align with recent updates in the WebSocket specification project. (markt) 

#### Tribes

*   ![Image 1172: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[#454](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/454): Differentiate warning messages in `KubernetesMembershipProvider` so that the missing attribute is clear to the user. PR provided by Hal Deadman. (markt) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 1173: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Switch from Cobertura to JaCoCo for code coverage as Cobertura does not support code coverage for code compiled for Java 11 onwards. It also removes the need to use a single thread to run the tests. (markt)

Tomcat was incorrectly requiring an `=` character after `bytes`. Fix based on pull request [#449](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/449) by Thierry Guérin. (markt)

This addresses various bugs that caused streams to incorrectly report that they had timed out waiting for an allocation from the connection flow control window. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1185: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65577](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65577): Fix a `AccessControlException` reporting when running an NIO2 connector with TLS enabled. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1186: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Reclassify TLS ciphers that use AESCCM8 as medium security rather than high security to align with recent changes in OpenSSL. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1187: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix an issue that caused some Servlet non-blocking API reads of the HTTP request body to incorrectly use blocking IO. (markt)

### 2021-09-10 Tomcat 10.1.0-M5 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1198: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Enable Tomcat to start if an (old) XML parser is configured that does not support `allow-java-encodings`. A warning will be logged if such an XML parser is detected. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1199: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Change the behaviour of custom error pages. If an error occurs after the response is committed, once the custom error page content has been added to the response the connection is now closed immediately rather than closed cleanly. i.e. the last chunk that marks the end of the response body is no longer sent. This acts as an additional signal to the client that the request experienced an error. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1200: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65479](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65479): When handling requests using JASPIC authentication, ensure that `PasswordValidationCallback.getResult()` returns the result of the password validation rather than always returning `false`. Fixed via pull request [#438](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/438) provided by Robert Rodewald. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1201: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Improve the reusability of the `UserDatabase` by adding intermediate concrete implementation classes and allowing to do partial database updates on `save`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1202: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor the authenticators to delegate the check for preemptive authentication to the individual authenticators where an authentication scheme specific check can be performed. Based on pull request [#444](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/444) by Robert Rodewald. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1203: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add a `UserDatabase` implementation as a superset of the `DataSourceRealm` functionality. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1204: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Make sure the dynamic Principal returned by `UserDatabaseRealm` stays up to date with the database contents, and add an option to have it be static, similar to the other realms. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1205: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add `derby-*.jar` to the list of JARs to skip when scanning for TLDs, web fragments and annotations. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1206: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[#447](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/447). Correct JPMS metadata for catalina.jar. Pull request provided by Hui Wang. (markt) 

#### Coyote

Also remove the Java interfaces to the APR/Native library that are not used by the OpenSSL integration for the NIO and NIO2 connectors. (markt)

### not released Tomcat 10.1.0-M3 (markt)

#### General

*   ![Image 1231: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update the minimum required Java version to Java 11. (markt) 

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1232: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Incremented the supported Jakarta Servlet version to 6.0 to align with the current development branch of the Jakarta Servlet specification. Plans have changed and the next iteration of the Servlet specification will be 6.0 rather than 5.1. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1233: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65411](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65411): Always close the connection when an uncaught `NamingException` occurs to avoid connection locking. Submitted by Ole Ostergaard. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1234: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65433](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65433): Correct a regression in the fix for [65397](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65397) where a `StringIndexOutOfBoundsException` could be triggered if the canonical path of the target of a symlink was shorter than the canonical path of the directory in which the symlink had been created. Patch provided by Cedomir Igaly. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1235: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif)[65443](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65443): Refactor the `CorsFilter` to make it easier to extend. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1236: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) To avoid unnecessary cache revalidation, do not add an HTTP `Expires` header when setting adding an HTTP header of `CacheControl: private`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1237: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor JULI's custom `LogManager`, the web application class loader implementation, the web resources implementation, the `JreLeakPreventionListener` implementation and the `StandardJarScanner` implementation to remove Java 8 specific code now that the minimum Java version has been increased to 11. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1238: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Remove all references to the endorsed standards override feature and the specifying of optional packages (extensions) in the manifest as these are not supported in Java 11. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1239: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) When writing an HTTP/2 response via sendfile (only enabled when `useAsyncIO` is true) the connection flow control window was sometimes ignored leading to various error conditions. sendfile now checks both the stream and connection flow control windows before writing. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1240: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add debug logging for writing an HTTP/2 response via sendfile. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1241: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct bugs in the HTTP/2 connection flow control management that meant it was possible for a connection to stall waiting for a connection flow control window update that had already arrived. Any streams on that connection that were trying to write when this happened would time out. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1242: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65448](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65448): When using TLS with NIO, it was possible for a blocking response write to hang just before the final TLS packet associated with the response until the connection timed out at which point the final packet would be sent and the connection closed. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1243: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65454](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65454): Fix a race condition that could result in a delay to a new request. The new request could be queued to wait for an existing request to finish processing rather than the thread pool creating a new thread to process the new request. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1244: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65460](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65460): Correct a regression introduced in the previous release in the change to reduce the number of small HTTP/2 window updates sent for streams. A logic error meant that small window updates for the connection were dropped. This meant that the connection flow window slowly reduced over time until nothing could be sent. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1245: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Remove NIO workarounds and code that is no longer needed with Java 11. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1246: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor the endpoints to remove Java 8 specific code now that the minimum Java version has been increased to 11. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 1247: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Add additional generics to the EL API to align with the latest changes in the EL specification project. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1248: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Enable EL lambda expressions to be coerced to functional interfaces. This is an implementation of a proposed extension to the Jakarta Expression Language specification. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1249: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor the EL API and implementation to remove Java 8 specific code now that the minimum Java version has been increased to 11. (markt) 

#### WebSocket

### 2021-07-02 Tomcat 10.1.0-M2 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1257: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor the `RemoteIpValve` to use the common utility method for list to comma separated string conversion. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1258: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor `JNDIRealm$JNDIConnection` so its fields are accessible to sub-classes of `JNDIRealm`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1259: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix serialization warnings in `UserDatabasePrincipal` reported by SpotBugs. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1260: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65397](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65397): Calls to `ServletContext.getResourcePaths()` no longer include symbolic links in the results unless `allowLinking` has been set to `true`. If a resource is skipped because of this change, a warning will be logged as this typically indicates a configuration issue. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1261: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65368](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65368): Improve handling of clean closes of inbound TLS connections. Treat them the same way as clean closes of non-TLS connections rather than as unknown errors. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1262: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Modify the HTTP/2 connector not to sent small updates for stream flow control windows to the user agent as, depending on how the user agent is written, this may trigger small writes from the user agent that in turn trigger the overhead protection. Small updates for stream flow control windows are now combined with subsequent flow control window updates for that stream to ensure that all stream flow control window updates sent from Tomcat are larger than `overheadWindowUpdateThreshold`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1263: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add additional debug logging to track the current state of the HTTP/2 overhead count that Tomcat uses to detect and close potentially malicious connections. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1264: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Many HTTP/2 requests from browsers will trigger one overhead frame and one non-overhead frame. Change the overhead calculation so that a non-overhead frame reduces the current overhead count by 2 rather than 1. This means that, over time, the overhead count for a well-behaved connection will trend downwards. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1265: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Change the initial HTTP/2 overhead count from `-10` to `-10 * overheadCountFactor`. This means that, regardless of the value chosen for `overheadCountFactor`, when a connection opens 10 overhead frames in a row will be required to trigger the overhead protection. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1266: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Increase the default `overheadCountFactor` from `1` to `10` and change the reduction in overhead count for a non-overhead frame from `-2` to `-20`. This allows for a larger range (0-20) to be used for `overheadCountFactor` providing for finer-grained control. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1267: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Modify the parsing of HTTP header values that use the `1#token` to ignore empty elements as per RFC 7230 section 7 instead of treating the presence of empty elements as an error. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1268: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Expand the unit tests for `HttpServlet.doHead()` and correct the flushing of the response buffer. The buffer used to behave as if it was one byte smaller than the configured size. The buffer was flushed (and the response committed if required) when the buffer was full. The buffer is now flushed (and the response committed if required) if the buffer is full and there is more data to write. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1269: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix an issue where concurrent HTTP/2 writes (or concurrent reads) to the same connection could hang and eventually timeout when async IO was enabled (it is enabled by default). (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 1270: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65387](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65387): Correct a regression in the fix for [65124](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65124) and restore the local definition of `out` for tags that implement `TryCatchFinally`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1271: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65390](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65390): Correct a regression in the fix for [65124](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65124) and restore code that was removed in error leading to JSP compilation failures in some circumstances. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1272: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update to the Eclipse JDT compiler 4.20. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1273: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for specifying Java 17 (with the value `17`) as the compiler source and/or compiler target for JSP compilation. If used with an Eclipse JDT compiler version that does not support these values, a warning will be logged and the latest supported version will used. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1274: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65377](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65377): Update the Java code generation for JSPs not to use the boxed primitive constructors as they have been deprecated in Java 9 and marked for future removal in Java 16. `valueOf()` is now used instead. (markt) 

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 1275: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor the `DigestAuthenticator` to reuse a shared `SecureRandom` instance rather than create a new one to generate the `cnonce` if required. (markt) 

#### Web applications

*   ![Image 1276: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65385](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65385): Correct the link in the documentation web application the Maven Central repository. (markt) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 1277: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Use JSign to integrate the build script with the code signing service to enable release builds to be created on Linux as well as Windows. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1278: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update the OWB module to Apache OpenWebBeans 2.0.23. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1279: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update the CXF module to Apache CXF 3.4.4. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1280: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65369](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65369) / [#422](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/422): Add the additional `--add-opens=...` options required for running Tomcat on Java 16 onwards to the `service.bat` script to align it with the other start-up scripts. PR provided by MCMicS. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1281: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to French translations. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1282: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Korean translations. (woonsan) 
*   ![Image 1283: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update JUnit to version 4.13.2. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1284: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update EasyMock to 4.3. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1285: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update Objenesis to 3.2. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1286: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update UnboundID to 6.0.0. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1287: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update CheckStyle to 8.43. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1288: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update SpotBugs to 4.2.3. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1289: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update OSGi annotations to 1.1.0. (markt) 

### 2021-06-15 Tomcat 10.1.0-M1 (markt)

#### General

*   ![Image 1290: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) This release contains all of the changes up to and including those in Apache Tomcat 10.0.6 plus the additional changes listed below. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1291: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Remove code previously marked for removal in Tomcat 10.1.x. (markt) 

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1292: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Incremented the supported Jakarta Servlet version to 5.1 to align with the current development branch of the Jakarta Servlet specification. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1293: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65301](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65301): `RemoteIpValve` will now avoid getting the local host name when it is not needed. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1294: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65308](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65308): NPE in JNDIRealm when no `userRoleAttribute` is given. (fschumacher) 
*   ![Image 1295: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif)[#412](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/412): Add commented out, sample users for the Tomcat Manager app to the default `tomcat-users.xml` file. Based on a PR by Arnaud Dagnelies. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1296: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif)[#418](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/418): Add a new option, `pass-through`, to the default servlet's `useBomIfPresent` initialization parameter that causes the default servlet to leave any BOM in place when processing a static file and not to use the BOM to determine the encoding of the file. Based on a pull request by Jean-Louis Monteiro. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1297: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[#419](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/419): When processing POST requests of type `multipart/form-data` for parts without a filename that are added to the parameter map in String form, check the size of the part before attempting conversion to String. Pull request provided by tianshuang. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1298: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Implement the new `Cookie` methods `setAttribute()`, `getAttribute()` and `getAttributes()` introduced in Servlet 6.0. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1299: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) AprLifecycleListener does not show dev version suffix for libtcnative and libapr. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 1300: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Refactor principal handling in `UserDatabaseRealm` using an inner class that extends `GenericPrincipal`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1301: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Enable the default `doHead()` implementation in `HttpServlet` to correctly handle responses where the content length needs to be represented as a long since it is larger than the maximum value that can be represented by an int. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1302: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid synchronization on roles verification for the memory `UserDatabase`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1303: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix the default `doHead()` implementation in `HttpServlet` to correctly handle responses where the Servlet calls `ServletResponse.reset()` and/or `ServletResponse.resetBuffer()`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1304: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix the default `doHead()` implementation in `HttpServlet` to correctly handle responses generated using the Servlet non-blocking API. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1305: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65303](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65303): Fix a possible `NullPointerException` if an error occurs on an HTTP/1.1 connection being upgraded to HTTP/2 or on a pushed HTTP/2 stream. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1306: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Simplify AprEndpoint socket bind for all platforms. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 1307: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65340](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65340): Add missing check for a negative return value for `Hpack.decodeInteger` in the `HpackDecoder`, which could cause a `NegativeArraySizeException` exception. Submitted by Thomas, and verified the fix is present in the donated hpack code in a further update. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1308: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Add debug logging for HTTP/2 HPACK header decoding. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1309: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct parsing of HTTP headers consisting of a list of tokens so that a header with an empty token is treated consistently regardless of whether the empty token is at the start, middle or end of the list of tokens. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1310: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Remove support for the `identity` transfer encoding. The inclusion of this encoding in RFC 2616 was an error that was corrected in 2001. Requests using this transfer encoding will now receive a 501 response. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1311: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Process transfer encoding headers from both HTTP 1.0 and HTTP 1.1 clients. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1312: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that if the transfer encoding header contains the `chunked`, that the `chunked` encoding is the final encoding listed. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 1313: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Incremented the supported Jakarta Expression Language version to 5.0 to align with the current development branch of the Jakarta Expression Language specification. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1314: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Review code used to generate Java source from JSPs and tags and remove code found to be unnecessary. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1315: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor use of internal `ChildInfo` class to use compile time type checking rather than run time type checking. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1316: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65124](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65124): Partial fix. When generating Java source code to call a tag handler, only define the local variable `JspWriter out` when it is going to be used. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1317: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Add generics to the EL 5.0 API to align with the current EL 5.0 development branch. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1318: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update the `web-fragment.xml` included in `jasper.jar` and `jasper-el.jar` to use the Servlet 5.0 schema. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1319: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Update JspC to generate `web.xml` and `web-fragment.xml` files using Servlet 5.0 schemas. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1320: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/code.gif) Remove the deprecated method `MethodExpression.isParmetersProvided()` from the EL API to align with the current EL 5.0 development branch. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1321: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65358](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65358): Improve expression language method matching for methods with varargs. Where multiple methods may match the provided parameters, the method that requires the fewest varargs is preferred. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1322: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif)[65332](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65332): Add a commented out section in `catalina.policy` that provides the necessary permissions to compile JSPs with javac when running on Java 9 onwards with a security manager. It is commented out as it will cause errors if used with earlier Java versions. (markt) 

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 1323: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65317](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65317): When using `permessage-deflate`, the WebSocket connection was incorrectly closed if the uncompressed payload size was an exact multiple of 8192. Based on a patch provided by Saksham Verma. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1324: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update the `web-fragment.xml` included in `tomcat-websocket.jar` to use the Servlet 5.0 schema. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1325: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65342](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65342): Correct a regression introduced with the fix for [65262](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65262) that meant Tomcat's WebSocket implementation would only work with Tomcat's implementation of the Jakarta WebSocket API. (markt) 

#### Web applications

*   ![Image 1326: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve the description of the `maxConnections` and `acceptCount` attributes in the Connector section of the documentation web application. (markt) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 1327: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to French translations. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1328: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Korean translations. (woonsan) 
*   ![Image 1329: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/fix.gif)[65362](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65362): Correct a regression in the previous release. The change to create OSGi `Require-Capability` sections in manifests for Jakarta API JARs manually rather than with bnd annotations did not add the necessary manual entries to the embedded JARs. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1330: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update the packaged version of the Tomcat Native Library to 1.2.30. Also update the minimum recommended version to 1.2.30. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1331: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-10.1-doc/images/update.gif) Update bnd to 7.2.0. (markt)
